<h3 class="entry-title td-module-title"><a href="https://www.teaparty.org/mexican-president-and-other-officials-sound-alarm-over-migrant-president-bidens-border-policy-462686/" rel="bookmark" title="Migrant President: Mexico Sounds Alarm Over Biden Policy">Migrant President: Mexico Sounds Alarm Over Biden Policy</a></h3>

								type: "POST",
								url: 'https://www.teaparty.org/wp-admin/admin-post.php?action=verify_v2_recaptcha',
								data: {
									token: token

							})
							.done(function(v) {
								let vr = JSON.parse(v);
								if (vr.success === true)

								let grr = document.getElementById('g-recaptcha-response');
								if (grr)
									grr.parentNode.removeChild(grr);

								return;
							});

				event.preventDefault();

				let success = '/confirm-subscription/';
				let error = '/error/';

				if (false)
					window.open(success);

				let data = {
					userId: 'e92c13eed9e727076a08b1bf5cdafcc9'

				let location_override = jQuery("#ew_subform_605e4af212961").attr('location-override') || '';				
				let email = jQuery("#ew_subform_605e4af212961 input.email").val();
				let contactId = jQuery("#ew_subform_605e4af212961 input.contactId").val();

				if (!false) {
					if (!EW.isEmail(email)) {
						alert("Invalid email");
						return false;
					}

					// blow out contact id since it was just overrided by email
					EW.removeItem('contactId');					
				}

				if (email) data.email = email;
				if (contactId) data.contactId = contactId;

				let url = decodeURIComponent(window.location.search.substring(1)),
					urlParams = url.split('&'),
					urlParam, 
					i;

				for (i = 0; i < urlParams.length; i++) {
					urlParam = urlParams[i].split('=');
					data[urlParam[0]] = urlParam[1];
				}

				jQuery('#ew_subform_605e4af212961 *').filter(':input').each(function(){
					if (this.type === 'radio' || this.type === 'checkbox') {
						if (jQuery(this).is(':checked')) {
							data[this.name] = jQuery(this).val();
						}
					}
					else
						data[this.name] = jQuery(this).val();
				});

				var custom_parameters = ''.split('|');
				custom_parameters.forEach(c => {
					if (!c) return;

					let v = EW.getItem(c);

						data[c] = EW.getItem(c);

				var protected = ''.split(',');

					location_override = location_override.replace('{' + key + '}', encodeURIComponent(data[key]));
					if (key && data[key] && !protected.some((p) => {return p.substring(3) === key;}))

						delete data[k];
				})

</style></div><style> </style></div><h2 class="td-block-title"><a class="td-pulldown-size" href="/about-us/">About Tea Party</a></h2></div><div class="wpb_wrapper wpb_text_column td_block_wrap td_block_wrap vc_column_text tdi_78_846 tagdiv-type td-pb-border-top td_block_template_10" data-td-block-uid="tdi_78_846"><div class="td-block-title-wrap"></div><div class="td-fix-index"><p>The <a href="https://www.teaparty.org/">Tea Party</a> are those who possess a strong belief in the Judeo-Christian values embedded in our great founding documents. We believe the responsibility of our beloved nation is etched upon the hearts of true Patriots from every race, religion, national origin, and walk of life sharing a common belief in the values which made and keep our beloved nation great. This belief led to the creation of the modern-day Tea Party.</p>
<p>Our millions of members consist of Republicans, Democrats, Libertarians, and Independents who identify with the premises set forth by the U.S. Constitution and we are striking a chord and ringing true with the American Spirit.</p>
<p>We stand by the Constitution as inherently conservative.</p>
<p><strong>We serve as a beacon to the masses who have lost their way, a light illuminating the path to the original intentions of our Founding Fathers.</strong></p>
<p>We must have a choir of voices declaring America must stand on the values which made us great, only then will the politically blind see and deaf hear! </p>
